***distel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:distel.html>distel</a> (83968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:distel.html>distel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thistil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þistilaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***distributie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributie</a> (15974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">distribution</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">distributio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">distribuere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to distribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A distribution, the act, process or an instance of distributing or being distributed, including the marketing and logistic senses of wide deliveries.</li>
<li>Publicly controlled assignment/delivery of restricted goods, notably under rationing.</li>
<li>An agency in charge of the above.</li>
<li>Physical transmission of motion or energy.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributiebedrijf</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributiebon</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributiedienst</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributiegoederen</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributiekantoor</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributienet</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributierol</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> (31)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thit</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a></i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>this (neuter); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> by.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>this</b> house</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>this</b> child</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this, this here
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>this</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:divisie.html>divisie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:divisies.html>divisies</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">division</span> (specific senses)
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a large military unit, usually with <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> 15,000 <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> and divided into <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brigades.html>brigades</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">business</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a section of a company</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a part of a sports competition</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the process or calculation of dividing numbers</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hyphen</span></li></ol>

***doctorandus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandus.html>doctorandus</a> (36180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandus.html>doctorandus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who will become a doctor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandus.html>doctorandus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandi.html>doctorandi</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandussen.html>doctorandussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctorandus.html>doctorandusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">doctoranda</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dode.html>dode</a> (1172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dode.html>dode</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a></b>)

<ol><li>A deceased person

<li>A casualty, victim of a fatal killing, illness, accident etc.</li></ol>

***doden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a> (445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dôden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dōden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daudijaną</i>. Compare English <i>deaden</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dode.html>dode</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a></i>.

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dodge</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Buiskap.jpg/150px-Buiskap.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Buiskap.jpg/225px-Buiskap.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Buiskap.jpg/300px-Buiskap.jpg 2x" data-file-width="395" data-file-height="387" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:dodger.html>Dodger</a> on a small sailing boat</div></div></div>

***doeg.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doeg.html>doeg</a> (19895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from the Dutch dialect <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zaans" class="extiw" title="w:Zaans">Zaans</a>, where <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doeg.html>doeg</a></i> means <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">doec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*duok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*dōk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***doel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doel</a> (975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelen.html>doele</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ditch that separated two fields</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*duola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōlijǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōlijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dale.html>dale</a>, valley</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dale.html>dale</a>, valley</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Likely, the initial meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> "ditch, pit" which shifted to "pile of earth" to "pile of earth used as target in a shooting range" to "shooting target" to "goal".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelen.html>doelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>aim, purpose</li>
<li>destination</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> goal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doelstelling.html>doelstelling</a> (30611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ten <a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set a task</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing, -ation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelstelling.html>doelstelling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelstellingen.html>doelstellingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelstelling.html>doelstellinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
